    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

    I was wondering too and also haven't read it. I think the secret is that the h finds out that she has a half-sister and the H was keeping it from her.<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">…more</a>
    I was wondering too and also haven't read it. I think the secret is that the h finds out that she has a half-sister and the H was keeping it from her. She also gets pregnant. I think that's what gets her to go back to him. <a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">(less)</a>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Rush and Blaire have the first three books in the series (too far books - and the fourth book is the first book but in Rush's POV and isn't required).<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Rush and Blaire have the first three books in the series (too far books - and the fourth book is the first book but in Rush's POV and isn't required). The rest of the rosemary beach series is about different couples that are friends with Rush and Blaire. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6165339-akanksha-s-ren?shelf=all-about-the-rant">all-about-the-rant</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6165339-akanksha-s-ren?shelf=baby-kid">baby-kid</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer479034801" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2294618978072775980"><b>3 ☆s I've got a Major Rush Crush!!~</b><br/><br/><i><b>“No. One. Comes. Before. You.”</b><br/>Make her believe that you stupid ass hat! Cause sure as hell I didn't believe it.</i><br/><br/>I <b>loved</b> this book <b>But</b> at the same time I was highly disappointed.<br/>I devoured it in 3 hours flat, from 3:30am to 6:30am. SO WORTH IT!! But I felt it getting over too quickly for me.. I wanted more, so many things were missing in this, so many loose ends were not tied and especially the ending.. I was like WTF. First only this book is tiny and then to top</span>
  <span id="freeText2294618978072775980" style="display:none"><b>3 ☆s I've got a Major Rush Crush!!~</b><br><br><i><b>“No. One. Comes. Before. You.”</b><br>Make her believe that you stupid ass hat! Cause sure as hell I didn't believe it.</i><br><br>I <b>loved</b> this book <b>But</b> at the same time I was highly disappointed.<br>I devoured it in 3 hours flat, from 3:30am to 6:30am. SO WORTH IT!! But I felt it getting over too quickly for me.. I wanted more, so many things were missing in this, so many loose ends were not tied and especially the ending.. I was like WTF. First only this book is tiny and then to top it all stuff wasn't complete.<br>I wanted it not to get over, maybe I just expected A LOT because the first book was SO BLOODY GOOD.. btw, The book was amazing but at the same time it was not..<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358088ra/709256.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="dissapointed" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Rush+Blaire+Sex = <i>*woot woot*</i> HOT!!<br>The dual pov always wins my heart over. I love knowing what the guy is thinking in time of drama!!~<br>The book had love hate confusion drama angst and amazing friendship and some hot sex. :P<br><br>But towards the end, things seemed very very very rushed, and the ending felt incomplete and abrupt to me.<br>So many things felt like they were unsolved, scattered. But now Abbi has announced that she will be writing a book 3 for them.. So *phew*<br>I think she rushed this book up a bit, it could have easily been longer and all the unsolved matter could have been fit in this. I hope she takes her time with the third book for Rush and Blaire and gives us another 5 Star book :D<br><br>I am going to re-read this book this week itself because it was too fucking short for my liking and I am pretty sad/mad/pissed/unhappy.<br><br><b>When I saw the book had come out hours early I was all.. "Omfg, Rush is here early!~"<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/486627.gif" width="220" height="130" alt="d" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Blaire's back in Bama with a bajo on her knee! She's heart broken.. nursing her wounds.. just trying to escape and then BOOM! A bomb drops! Then the story begins!<br><br>Blaire Blaire Blaire!!!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400461i/776070.jpg" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>One thing I loved the most about this book, Like more than anything.. More than Rush too was <u>WOODS!!<u></u></u></b> He is like THE BEST.<br>Then I fell in love with Woods all over again, I mean I just cannot wait for his book to learn more about him!! He's the sweetest person everr!!<br><br>I loveee Bethy, amazing friend and sweet chick! :)<br><br>Then in the middle of the book, all I could think about was how good this is and I was all giddy happy for Blaire and Rush! I mean her preggy hormones were doing wonders for Rush and us readers too!! ;)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/606781.gif" width="430" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The chemistry, sizzle and sex was ozzing hotness!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401074ra/777865.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380743099ra/3118141.gif" width="380" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380743099ra/3118142.gif" width="400" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then I got pissed, Because things were going nowhere and I wanted to beat the shit out of Rush.. I swear he is a stupid stupid jerk!!!! This book was a bit dragged out.. I mean the same book1 drama was being dragged out here.. Nothing new was developing.. Blaire would Run, Rush would follow.. When Rush would run.. Blaire would be like 'I'm insecure'<br>Well.. FUCK YOU ALL.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/627579.gif" width="250" height="175" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I wanted to yell at him to get his fucking head out of his ass and just think straight!!<br>You got to do right by your woman man, I mean stand up for her, stand by her and be the fuck there.. talk shit, love her and make her believe she fucking comes first. Not run off at the first bumpy road. JERK.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401074ra/777866.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Just reading about Nan and her god awful mother was making my blood boil, I hate those bitches with all my being. Such a selfish fucking sluts. Abe too. Spineless bastard.</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401074ra/777867.gif" width="320" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/454588.gif" width="320" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I wanted a lot more out of this book, there was barely any scene in Rush's house.. I wanted more stuff about Cain too.<br> <br><b>
  <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There was barely anything about the pregnancy!! I mean yes she was pregnant ok, but I wanted more out of that, more about Rush's feelings about that!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>
</b><br>All we saw here was he was angry, then he was a hot mess then he was all over Blaire ;) ;) :) Then he was a wuss then he became normal.<br><br>There was not a lot about Rush's mom or Abe, I was expecting more drama there.. Even with Nan, I just expected a wayh lot more.. About a lot of things!!!<br>A lot of things left unfinished between many characters in this book..<br><br>I loveddddd Woods Bethy Grant and Ryan! Such nice characters..<br>But something seemed off about Grant too.. but we'll wait for his book and see.. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[If Nan is the lead in her book, I will hate Grant as much as I hate Nan, the mother and Abe. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>About the ending.. </b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I was pissed how Abe openly admitted how spineless he was that he couldn't do right by his OWN wife and kid. THAT HE WOULD RUN AWAY AT THEIR TIME OF NEED AND GO FUCKING PLAY FAMILY WITH SOMEONE ELSES KID AND FAMILY. BASTARD.<br>I was pissed with Rush for just leaving Blaire for a week with no fucking word what so ever and then when he was back, Blaire took him back without a word. STUPID SPINELESS!!<br>And Rush lost all his badboy.ness which all of us fell for in book1.. I mean where were your balls man?? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>I love you Abbi, Thank you for giving us so many books in this series because I totally loved all the characters</b> except Nan, the mother and Abe.<br><b>The story is magnificent, and your writing ROCKS but I just expected a lot more!!! Can't wait for the rest of your amazing books to come out this year. ;D </b><br><br>Hope the rest of the 3 books in the series are as amazing as the first book! :P<br>Btw, at the end of all this drama... I still love Rush and Blaire. and Woods the most! ;)<br><br>Now... there is a Bonus chapter, go find it here on Abbi's page andddddd..<br>Ta Ta Ta Ta.. WE ARE GETTING ONE MORE RUSH &amp; BLAIRE BOOK if you guys already didn't know.. hehe :)<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401074ra/777868.gif" width="380" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_489556735" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/489556735" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/489556735?book_show_action=true">Dec 30, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer489556735" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5826587743583573633"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402640i/782748._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>4.5 stars <br/><br/><i> <b> “No. One. Comes. Before. You.” </b> </i><br/><br/>I HEART RUSH!! and I loved this book!<br/><br/><b> Ohhhh this book was just so <u> ADDICTIVE </u> !!! There is something about Abbi Glines’ writing that makes me desperately just want more and more and more!!!<br/><br/>Its the kind of story you can just inhale in one sitting – a quick, deliciously angsty, drama-filled romance. </b><br/><br/>What made me love it was that I never once, not for one second EVER EVER EVER doubted how right Blaire and Rush were for each other, or how much they loved e</span>
  <span id="freeText5826587743583573633" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402640i/782748._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>4.5 stars <br><br><i> <b> “No. One. Comes. Before. You.” </b> </i><br><br>I HEART RUSH!! and I loved this book!<br><br><b> Ohhhh this book was just so <u> ADDICTIVE </u> !!! There is something about Abbi Glines’ writing that makes me desperately just want more and more and more!!!<br><br>Its the kind of story you can just inhale in one sitting – a quick, deliciously angsty, drama-filled romance. </b><br><br>What made me love it was that I never once, not for one second EVER EVER EVER doubted how right Blaire and Rush were for each other, or how much they loved each other. That was clear and unwavering. That being said, they went through some pretty serious ups and downs, huge insecurities, a lot of mess ups and dysfunctionality along their road to making their relationship work.<br><br>At times it was a little ‘much’ for me, but I got the same feeling while reading this book that I get when I’m watching a really well-written TV show — its like, I know that sometimes its just “drama” but I just eat it up!<br><br>I’m not going to talk about the plot of this one at all. Its a direct continuation of book #1 "<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16070903.Fallen_Too_Far__Too_Far___1_" title="Fallen Too Far (Too Far, #1) by Abbi Glines" rel="nofollow noopener">Fallen Too Far</a>" (which should absolutely be read first) and the story picks up 3 weeks after the cliffhanger ending of the first one. There’s a bit of a twist that I suspected from book one that plays out in this book and basically affects the whole general story line. I loved it and loved where it took the characters.<br><br>The story was told in chapter-by-chapter alternating POVs so we were never left too long without understanding both sides of the story.<br><br>I seriously seriously seriously love Rush. That guy just makes my heart race. He’s hot, swoony, and flawed (not to mention tattooed and pierced). Just… gah! How can you not love him when he says stuff like this:<br><br><i> <b> “There is nothing is rather do than be near you… [I'll] take whatever the hell I can get when it comes to you… I will do anything. Anything, Blaire, just to be near you… You need me, I’m there.” </b></i> <br><br>For the most part I really liked the way he handled things – I mean, sure he kept messing up and I wanted to grab him by the shoulders and shake him a few times but his mistakes were mostly understandable, and let me tell you, that man knew how to grovel. There was just no way you could doubt his intentions. I mean this was all new to him too – the first time he’d actually cared about someone enough to want a relationship… his first time actually falling in love.<br><br>It totally warmed my heart how he was never willing to just let any of their issues go. He tried to respect her space but at the same time was always pushing to try and work through them. You could just FEEL how much he was desperately head-over-heels in love with Blaire and you just KNEW that he’d do just about anything to protect her.<br><br><i> <b> “Let me prove it to you. Leaving me doesn’t let me prove anything. You have to stay with me, Blaire. You have to give me a chance… Trust me to protect you and put you first.” </b> </i><br><br>My heart just plain HURT when he messed up, or when unfortunate situations lead to misunderstanding and general angst but at the same time I love the feel that it gave the story – it kept you a little worried and yet totally invested in the character’s lives.<br><br><i> “I love you, Blaire. I love you so damn much it hurts.” </i> <br><br>I felt bad for Blaire because for the most part, I understood her insecurities – about not being a part of his world, being reminded of it every day and being surrounded by reasons why they wouldn’t fit together. I liked that she wasn’t weak – she simply had trust issues brought on by all the men in her life, in some way or another, betraying her. And given Rush’s past and his family connections, it was hard for her to accept that she could actually put stock in his love for her.<br><br><i> “She’d lost everyone in her life she’d love and trusted. Why would she believe me? The only men in her life had left her. Betrayed her. She expected nothing else… I wasn’t letting anyone else hurt her.” </i><br><br><i> <b> “I love her. I will stop at nothing to make sure she’s safe.” </b></i> <br><br>There is some serious hotness in this book – much like in the first one. Some of those scenes had me fanning myself! Definitely adult.<br><br>And, rest easy! There is no cliffhanger at the end of this book!!! *whew* But, that being said, you are left wanting ‘more’. It leaves off at a happy place, but it was a bit abrupt. I would have definitely loved an epilogue or just a tiny glimpse into their future but I know there are going to be two more books in this series so, despite them not being focused on Blaire and Rush, I have high hopes of seeing more of them in the future and maybe of getting a giant swoony epilogue at the end of the whole series :)<br><br><i> <b> “No man has ever loved a woman as much as I love you. Nothing will ever come before you. I don’t know what else I have to do to prove to you that I won’t let you down again. I won’t hurt you. You don’t have to be alone anymore. I need you.” </b></i> <br><br>I absolutely LOVED this book and I would definitely recommend this series for everyone!<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16070903.Fallen_Too_Far__Too_Far___1_" title="Fallen Too Far (Too Far, #1) by Abbi Glines" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1349565157s/16070903.jpg" alt="Fallen Too Far (Too Far, #1) by Abbi Glines" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17029526.Never_Too_Far__Too_Far___2_" title="Never Too Far (Too Far, #2) by Abbi Glines" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1356822956s/17029526.jpg" alt="Never Too Far (Too Far, #2) by Abbi Glines" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402640i/782749._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="5826587743583573633" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8615049478244415098">Review posted at: <a href='http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/?m=1' rel='nofollow noopener'> Swept Away By Romance</a> <br/><br/><b>2 1/2 stars</b><br/><br/>I had such high hopes for this book but ultimately felt let down. I was disappointed in Rush and Blaire's characters. They didn't have the same presence in this book that they had in the first. They felt robbed of the essence that made them unique and intriguing in the first story. They became carbon copies of the stereotypical hero and heroine whose actions and behavior were totally predictable. Unlike the first book, its sequel felt contrived</span>
  <span id="freeText8615049478244415098" style="display:none">Review posted at: <a href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/?m=1" rel="nofollow noopener"> Swept Away By Romance</a> <br /><br /><b>2 1/2 stars</b><br /><br />I had such high hopes for this book but ultimately felt let down. I was disappointed in Rush and Blaire's characters. They didn't have the same presence in this book that they had in the first. They felt robbed of the essence that made them unique and intriguing in the first story. They became carbon copies of the stereotypical hero and heroine whose actions and behavior were totally predictable. Unlike the first book, its sequel felt contrived and somewhat manufactured. For me, what was once original and refreshing became simply run-of-the mill. It saddened me. <br /><br />I felt the true star of this story was Wood. I fell in love with him and looked forward with anticipation to his scenes. He jumped off the pages and shined brilliantly. I'm very much looking forward to reading his book. <br /><br />While this particular story did not work for me, I can see why readers are drawn to it. Abbi Glines is one talented author. <br /><br /><b>Note: I heard there will be another book for Rush and Blaire. I'm sure fans of this story are ecstatic about this news, but in all honesty, this story is DONE. Why not give the readers a few reasonably priced vignettes? They're a fabulous way for authors to give their readers more of the characters they want and love while not jeopardizing the authenticity of their story. Just a thought.</b></span>

<div id="review_549349079" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/549349079" />
    <a title="Dd" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9444787-dd"><img alt="Dd" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/549349079?book_show_action=true">Mar 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dd" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dd" href="/user/show/9444787-dd">Dd</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer549349079" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18083804849367035558"><br/><b>So Readers,do you know who's grinning like a fool right now???</b><br/><br/><i>Yup,that's me!!!Sorry,can't help it.</i><br/><br/><b>Because of Rushhhhhh.......</b><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Yeah,yeah, I know he worships Blaire.But a girl can dream,right??</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>Enough said, now about this story....</i><br/><br/>---------------------------------------------------------<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"He wasn't what sent me running.He was what made me want to stay."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Warning - Please proceed only if you have read the 1st book of this series...Fallen Too Far.<br/><br/><br/>This book starts where Fallen Too Far left off....</span>
  <span id="freeText18083804849367035558" style="display:none"><br /><b>So Readers,do you know who's grinning like a fool right now???</b><br /><br /><i>Yup,that's me!!!Sorry,can't help it.</i><br /><br /><b>Because of Rushhhhhh.......</b><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Yeah,yeah, I know he worships Blaire.But a girl can dream,right??</i>
</b><br /><br /><i>Enough said, now about this story....</i><br /><br />---------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"He wasn't what sent me running.He was what made me want to stay."</i>
</b><br /><br />Warning - Please proceed only if you have read the 1st book of this series...Fallen Too Far.<br /><br /><br />This book starts where Fallen Too Far left off.....<br /><br /><b>With Blaire's entire world crashed and shattered.<br /><br />With Rush's one broken and empty.</b><br /><br /><b>
  <pre>Blaire is ready to forgive, but how can she <br />forget???</pre>
</b><br /><i>All the lies.<br /><br /><br />All the pain.<br /><br /><br />How can she forget that Rush had chosen Nan over her??</i><br /><br /><br />She is trying to pick up the pieces when suddenly her world twists once again and leaves her careening.<br /><br /><b>Something unexpected happens.</b><br /><br /><b>
  <pre>And she might just discover that no matter <br />how far you try to run,it might be......</pre>
</b><br /><b>NEVER TOO FAR!!!</b><br /><br /><br />The best part of this story was Rush's POV. At least for me.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"It had been three weeks, four days and twelve hours since I'd seen her. Since she'd torn my heart out."</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />When he had taken her in,he had not expected her to own his heart.Own his very soul.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I don't just love her,she owns me.Completely.I'd do anything for her."</i>
</b><br /><br />And now that he has lost her,he's ready to do anything to get her back.<br /><br /><i>Push, pull, demand, beg,.......<br /><br />........anything!!</i><br /><br /><br />So,can they ever get back what they had???<br /><br />That passion,that flame,that love.....<br /><br /><br />Read it to find out!!!<br /><br />------------------------------------------------------<br /><br />Now,my heart grieves,but I have to point out what I did not like.Otherwise it won't be fair.<br /><br />Like the first book,this one too was very easy to read.It had enough twists and new angles to keep me interested.It was fast paced too.<br /><br />But what bothered me was sheer dumb decisions made by the characters.<br /><br />I think Woods was the only rational character in there.Really.Oh and by the way I can't wait to read Woods story next.**sqeee** I think I'm already in love with him.Though I'm not very sure about Meg.And...I'm veering off the topic.<br /><br /><b>So yes,as I was saying,I did not like their stupid, impulsive, irrational decisions at all.</b><br /><br />I'm not adding any spoilers but really I could not help feeling that they were getting a little too melodramatic sometimes.<br /><br /><b>Yeah,all the woe of this world belongs to you,I get it.I sympathize. But it does get a bit tiring after sometime.</b><br /><br /><br /><i>But it's okay.I still enjoyed it.</i><br /><br /><br />And the sweet moments made up for it!!<br /><br /><br />The ending was sooooo cute.I loved it.But I wanted more.<br /><br /><br /><b>Good news,I think everyone knows it by now,still....we're getting a third book!!!!</b><br /><br /><br />----------------------------------------------------<br /><br />Okay one more thing.....I STILL HATE NAN!!!<br /><br />She is a brat and I do not mean it in a good way.She's dumb and quite frankly still a bitch.<br /><br />What the hell is up with Grant???? I like him.But why is he taking Nan's side all of a sudden???<br /><br />This better not be what I think it will be.<br /><br /><b>Grant + Nan = Aaarghhh!!!!</b><br /><br />Huh,let's see!!<br /><br /><br /><br /><b>That's all for now,Readers!!<br /><br />Ta-Ta!!!</b><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="18083804849367035558" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_480590292" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/480590292" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/480590292?book_show_action=true">Dec 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=author-abbi-glines">author-abbi-glines</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer480590292" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12349160298886683676"><b>
  <i>“She’s amazing. No… she’s perfect. Everything about her is fucking perfect...I don’t just love her, she owns me. Completely. I'd do anything for her.” </i>
</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>Never Too Far picks up exactly where we left Blaire in Fallen Too Far. She staying at Granny Q’s house with her ex-boyfriend Cain in Alabama. We soon find out that she is expecting and has no plans of rekindling her relationship with Cain but is at a loss as to what to do next. Blaire visits her mom and sister at the cemetery and </span>
  <span id="freeText12349160298886683676" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“She’s amazing. No… she’s perfect. Everything about her is fucking perfect...I don’t just love her, she owns me. Completely. I'd do anything for her.” </i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Never Too Far picks up exactly where we left Blaire in Fallen Too Far. She staying at Granny Q’s house with her ex-boyfriend Cain in Alabama. We soon find out that she is expecting and has no plans of rekindling her relationship with Cain but is at a loss as to what to do next. Blaire visits her mom and sister at the cemetery and she receives her answer...Bethy!!!! Love this girl! She is a great friend and makes Blaire an offer that she can’t refuse.<br><br>Blaire is secure in her plan to keep Rush as a friend even though she loves him. She feels that Rush will always choose his mother and sister first.<br> <br><b>
  <i>“His sister hated me. His mother hated me. They hated my mother. And I hated my father. For Rush to be a part of this baby’s life he’d have to give them up. I couldn’t ask him to give up his mom and sister. Even if they were evil. He loved them.”</i>
</b><br><br>Rush will do anything to be near Blaire. He is a man in love and tries so hard to show Blaire that she can count on him. Rush lays the law down to Nan, he tells her to back off or she will loss all of his financial support as well as him. When he learns of the baby he is hell bent on protecting what’s his. <br> <br>Nan remains the bitchy redheaded sister who is hell bent on squashing Blaire only this time Rush is having none of it. <br><br>Rush is once again all sorts of hot and alpha in this sequel. He has to learn quickly how to be in a relationship. He stumbles along the way but the fact remains that he will do anything for Blaire. Here is my one Rush complaint...Pick up your damn phone, he could have called while he sat vigil by Nan. The internal struggle between his sister and his future had me crazy. Rush quickly gets back on track with a little guidance from a surprise source. He is one hot man in love!<br><br>Grant switches sides one to many times for me in this book. I even felt that he may have been the secret lover at the condo. <br> <br>Woods is the MAN! He never sways in his loyalty, love and friendship. He protects Blaire throughout this book make no mistake he loves her but from the get go does the right thing by her. He appears to play the middle letting Rush know the score but a reader knows he does it out of love for Blaire. Saying that I’m excited for his book is an understatement! <br> <br><b>
  <i>“If you aren’t going after her I am. She needs someone right now. As much as I don’t want it to be you because I don’t think you deserve her it needs to be you.”</i>
</b>~Woods<br><br>Yes this reader is Team Woods and I can’t wait till he gets the girl! <br><br>I wish there was epilogue or that the book was longer. I would have liked a scene between Nan and Blaire once Nan found out the truth. I want that wench on her knees with apologies or presents!<br><br>Overall, I couldn’t get enough of these great characters and I enjoyed every minute of this book. I read it in one sitting so that has to say something. Rush and Blaire were very HOT and STEAMY and the book left me very happy!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380361470i/712480._SX540_.jpg" width="320" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12349160298886683676" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_497026448" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/497026448" />
    <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews"><img alt="Tough Critic Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345668583p2/5336035.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/497026448?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews?shelf=march-2013">march-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer497026448" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10139133729294851695">Dear Abbi Glines,<br/><br/>So after reading <i>Never Too Far</i> I needed to correspond and let you know that you've once again squashed my indifference. It wasn't immediately squashed in <i>Fallen Too Far</i>. In fact, I have yet to rate it. I <i>really</i> liked it, but I couldn't seem to put a star with my thoughts. Some things in that book just happened a little too fast and if I'm going to be honest here, Rush's "sweet Blaire" started to creep me out a little. I tried to hear it all sweet and sexy, but it all kept soundi</span>
  <span id="freeText10139133729294851695" style="display:none">Dear Abbi Glines,<br /><br />So after reading <i>Never Too Far</i> I needed to correspond and let you know that you've once again squashed my indifference. It wasn't immediately squashed in <i>Fallen Too Far</i>. In fact, I have yet to rate it. I <i>really</i> liked it, but I couldn't seem to put a star with my thoughts. Some things in that book just happened a little too fast and if I'm going to be honest here, Rush's "sweet Blaire" started to creep me out a little. I tried to hear it all sweet and sexy, but it all kept sounding very Hannibal Lector-ish. I got over it though! I got over it and then I got <i>under</i> Rush. Holy hot hell and flaming panties batman! You took it to a new level. <i>Fallen Too Far</i> ended on a very high note and I couldn't wait for the sequel<br /><br />Now with the risk of making <i>Fallen Too Far</i> feel like the red headed step child, I thought <i>Never Too Far</i> blew it away. Speaking of blowing. Rush's oral fixation. What the hell!? I'm surprised he didn't just take a straw to Blaire's lady bits. It was so deliciously naughty (Pun intended, pun definitely intended). <br /><br />I also need to hug your face for not drawing out "the chase" or exhausting the "will she, won't she". You handled everything perfectly. I might even turn a trick or two because you didn't love triangle us! Nothing is more annoying than a girl's constant in<b>dick</b>cision. Thank God!!<br /><br />I'm pretty sure you didn't mean for the, "These titties are mine..." comment to be funny, but I was in tears. Literal tears. Purposeful or not, it provided great comic release...I mean relief. Rush pulled off the dirty talk and when he didn't pull it off, he pulled it off by coming across as funny. He was the perfect oxy moron.<br /><br />This book was 4.5~stars and I thought the pace was perfect. No draggy bits, no skimmage. I was hooked. Overall the series was 4~stars, but four very orgasmic stars. I cannot wait to get a peek when you finally do ADULT! This was pretty damn close so I can only imagine. I hope we get more of Blaire and Rush in the other books because I'm pretty sure I wasn't ready for it to end. Where in the hell was my epilogue ;-)<br /><br />I may have started out riding the fence with this series, but you yanked me over and smacked some sense into me. Thank you for that and thank you for this series. WRITE ON!<br /><br />Sincerely, <br /><br />Your Reader<br /><br />More at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blogspot.com">www.toughcriticbookreviews.blogspot.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10139133729294851695" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText5352557765929544761" style="display:none"><b> Update March 3 </b><br>Maybe I just had my hope up way way high. Maybe that's why I ended up giving it 4 stars instead of 5. <div id="review_480028606" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/480028606" />
    <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie"><img alt="Natasha is a Book Junkie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585046882p2/9389992.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/480028606?book_show_action=true">Dec 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natasha is a Book Junkie" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie">Natasha is a Book Junkie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer480028606" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15745949255319496526"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“No man has ever loved a woman as much as I love you. Nothing will ever come before you.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>Rarely does a sequel to a book you’ve loved and re-read more times than you wish to admit ever live up to its high expectations – you’re afraid the plotline would be thin, the characters taken in a direction you don’t wish them to be taken, the overall ‘feeling’ of the book not as intensely or consistently pieced together. Well, you have absolutely no reason to fear any of that when it comes to t</span>
  <span id="freeText15745949255319496526" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“No man has ever loved a woman as much as I love you. Nothing will ever come before you.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />Rarely does a sequel to a book you’ve loved and re-read more times than you wish to admit ever live up to its high expectations – you’re afraid the plotline would be thin, the characters taken in a direction you don’t wish them to be taken, the overall ‘feeling’ of the book not as intensely or consistently pieced together. Well, you have absolutely no reason to fear any of that when it comes to this book because Abbi Glines has just helped me achieve a new level of ‘book junkie nirvana’. Never Too Far is EVERYTHING I have hoped it would be and then some.<br /><br />After the traumatic cliffhanger we were left with at the end of Fallen Too Far, both our beloved characters are emotional train wrecks. Blaire has run away from Rosemary and from the man she loves, and is hoping to find solace in the familiarity of her home town. She is left with nothing in life, no possessions, no plans for the future, no family that she can rely on to help her heal her shattered soul. She craves to have a family again, to feel unconditional love again, to mean something to someone. Everything she has always believed to be true has been shaken, questioned, attacked, and we find our gentle heroine heartbroken and alone.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I don’t want to be alone… but I am. And I'm scared.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Rush is battling his own demons after Blaire’s departure. For the first time in his life he has fallen in love with someone body and soul, and for the first time in his life he wants to put her well-being first, before anyone else’s, including his sister Nan’s. His last encounter with Blaire has scarred him deeply because he saw the real effects of what his family had done to her. The memory of her vacant eyes haunt him, torture him and don’t allow him to move on. His guilt for the role he played in Blaire’s heartbreak stop him from going after her again, deep down hoping she would come back to him in her own time.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“She may have had enough time to deal with things. What if she does come back? What will you do?”<br />What would I do?<br />I’d beg.</i>
</blockquote><br />But life is not done throwing them curveballs and very soon Blaire is forced to return to Rosemary, albeit temporarily, and attempt to find her place in the world again. She leaves the safety of her past once more, trading the familiar comforts of her home town for the unknown of a world that has treated her only badly. She bravely takes control of her life and goes back to the one place that broke her.<br /><br />So what happens when you throw a starving man a bone? He clenches to it and never wants to let go. Blaire’s return has given Rush hope, but he is fearful of scaring Blaire off and making her run away from him again. So he threads carefully, giving her space and time, but his heart and body naturally gravitate towards her and the pull is too irresistible to fight. We see a desperate man, a man who is deeply in love with the woman before him but doesn’t know how to make her trust him again. His desperation is heart-wrenching, playing with our emotions every time we hear his voice and his most intimate thoughts about Blaire. He tries to control his emotions when he’s around her, but his every touch, glance in her direction, need to be as close to her physically as possible give them away.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I will do anything. Anything, Blaire, just to be near you. I can’t think about anything else. I can’t focus on anything.”</i>
</blockquote><br />These young lovers are faced with a reality that sets its own pace, making them aware that time is not necessarily something they can freely fritter away. Their biggest obstacle is not the love that binds them together – it is the lack of trust between them. Blaire finds it hard to trust him because all the men that meant anything to her in her life had abandoned her when she needed them the most. She expects Rush to do the same. She accepts it and considers it to be inevitable. But while Blaire might have more tangible reasons for not trusting Rush again with her heart, Rush is unconsciously distrustful of Blaire as well because he is constantly expecting her to bolt. He does not feel worthy of her and he keeps failing her because of that.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I wondered how many more times I was going to screw up before I ever got this right.”</i>
</blockquote><br />While Fallen Too Far was ‘Blaire’s book’ because we only heard her voice, Never To Far is no longer only her story. By giving us both points of view and by allowing us to hear Rush’s thoughts as well, he truly becomes ‘our’ hero. We feel for him, we understand him, we struggle with his own inner conflicts. Ms Glines has given us the perfect man to pine after and he is spectacular, inside and out.<br /><br />The secondary characters are developed even more this time around, we get to know them better, see what motivates their actions and fall in love with a few of them. Especially the one that is getting his own book next – Woods.<br /><br />This is a book about a love that is all-consuming, a devotion that is truly inspiring, a physical connection that will make your toes curl every time Blaire and Rush share a scene in the story. You will fall in love with these characters all over again and you’ll become invested in them even more. Beautifully paced, skilfully written, I loved every single delicious moment of it.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“She’s amazing. No… she’s perfect. Everything about her is f*cking perfect … I don’t just love her, she owns me. Completely. I'd do anything for her.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />~ N ♥<br /><br /><a href="http://www.natashaisabookjunkie.com/2013/02/23/never-too-far-by-abbi-glines/" rel="nofollow noopener">See this review on my blog!</a> | <a href="http://www.facebook.com/natashaisabookjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Facebook!</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15745949255319496526" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_503817804" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/503817804" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/503817804?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="xrysa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="xrysa" href="/user/show/9016476-xrysa">xrysa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9016476-xrysa?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer503817804" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2459206471261653732">I expected this to be awesome , like the first book.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358088ra/709255.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Unfortunatelly , it wasn't.<br/><br/><b>Blaire</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404769i/787931._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Blaire ,in the beginning of this books , is living at Cain's grandmother's house.She is suspicious that something is wrong with her and her fear comes alive. <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[She is pregnant. <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/>Her best friend Bethy missed her and she is visiting her in Alabama , in order to make up her mind and make her return to Rosemary.<br/>After an incident,she has to go to Rosemary and face Rush.<br/><br/><b>Rush</b><br/> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404769i/787932.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>We are introduce</span>
  <span id="freeText2459206471261653732" style="display:none">I expected this to be awesome , like the first book.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358088ra/709255.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Unfortunatelly , it wasn't.<br><br><b>Blaire</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404769i/787931._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Blaire ,in the beginning of this books , is living at Cain's grandmother's house.She is suspicious that something is wrong with her and her fear comes alive. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[She is pregnant. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>Her best friend Bethy missed her and she is visiting her in Alabama , in order to make up her mind and make her return to Rosemary.<br>After an incident,she has to go to Rosemary and face Rush.<br><br><b>Rush</b><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404769i/787932.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We are introduced a new version of this guy.<br><i>He is not a bad boy anymore</i>...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380366954ra/719345.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4872191.Abbi_Glines" title="Abbi Glines" rel="nofollow noopener">Abbi Glines</a> we liked that douche bag .<br>I cant argue I have a thing for broken hearted guys but seeing Rush like that didn't affect me at all.<br>Fortunatelly , this bad boy returned at the second half of the book but then I was starting getting irritated by Blaire.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404769ra/787933.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Jesus sweetheart , you were <b>TOO</b> jealous!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404769ra/787934.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Woods</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404769i/787935.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404769ra/787936.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He supported Blaire and he completely understood that he shouldt try again with her because her heart belong to Rush.<br><br><b>Nan</b><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404769ra/787937.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She is awful!<br>I'm afraid that if she ever bites her tongue , she will die from her own venom.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404769i/787938.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Some good quotes</i><br><br><b>“No. One. Comes. Before You.”</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404769ra/787939.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“Listen to me, Blaire. If you try to go anywhere I will chase you down. I will become your shadow. I won't let you out of my sight because I can't live without you. I made so many damn mistakes with you I don't even want to try and count them but I am going to start making things right from here on out.”</b><br><br><b>“She may have had enough time to deal with things. What if she does come back? What will you do?" Grant asked me.<br><br>What would I do?<br><br>I'd beg.”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404769ra/787940.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Finally,my favorite part were the couple last chapters.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I was afraid during the whole book that something will happen and she will lose the baby and reading these chapters made me feel relief.I'm so glad he didnt toss her away and he took his responsibility. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I think their story is over and there is no need for the author to write a third book about them.<br>I'm anxiously awaiting for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17333880.Twisted_Perfection__Too_Far___3_" title="Twisted Perfection (Too Far, #3) by Abbi Glines" rel="nofollow noopener">Twisted Perfection</a>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404769ra/787941.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_488885509" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/488885509" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/488885509?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer488885509" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3677331957092268822"><b>3/3 ~ Never Too Far bonus chapter:<br/><br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.abbiglines.com/2013/03/673/'>http://www.abbiglines.com/2013/03/673/</a></b><br/><br/><br/>I just want to start out saying that I LOVE Rush. I think he's a great character...he has all the 'goodies' and he's matured so much. I really enjoyed how he went after Blaire and how much he tempered himself and tried to respect her wishes. <br/><br/>But....I was really disappointed. There are two instances in the book where it seems to be out of character for him. The first one is understandable ~ maybe ~ but the second one, I just </span>
  <span id="freeText3677331957092268822" style="display:none"><b>3/3 ~ Never Too Far bonus chapter:<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.abbiglines.com/2013/03/673/">http://www.abbiglines.com/2013/03/673/</a></b><br><br><br>I just want to start out saying that I LOVE Rush. I think he's a great character...he has all the 'goodies' and he's matured so much. I really enjoyed how he went after Blaire and how much he tempered himself and tried to respect her wishes. <br><br>But....I was really disappointed. There are two instances in the book where it seems to be out of character for him. The first one is understandable ~ maybe ~ but the second one, I just can't get over. I mean, <i>come on people</i>, <b>SEVEN</b> days?? What in the heck was up with that?? Hats off to Blaire even though she was at the end of her rope. I really think a phone call would have gone a long way. Ugh...it just makes me sick and it's so hard to be disgusted with him.<br><br>And what can I say about Blaire? She's still a spitfire but it kills me that what she went through in the last book has shaken her self confidence. She questions e-v-e-r-y-t-h-i-n-g...some things are understandable but sometimes, it was a bit too much. <br><br>Thank goodness for the shining stars of the book: Bethy, Woods and Grant. I loved when Bethy showed up in the cemetery and was always there for Blaire. That didn't mean she didn't show her some tough love when she needed it! Woods is really amazing. In the first book, he could've been a bit of a creeper but he has really stepped up to the plate. I Can. Not. Wait. for his book! Grant is still the good guy but something is a bit different with him. I can't quite put my finger on it but OMG...I hope it has <i>nothing</i> to do with Nan!! <br><br>Rush + Blaire = some very steamy scenes. I think the hotness level was ramped up a few degrees....phewwww! <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Blaire, tell me what you want me to do. I’ll do whatever it is you need.”</i>
</blockquote> <br><blockquote>
  <i>“You’re driving me crazy, Blaire. Insane, baby. F*cking insane.”</i>
</blockquote> <br><blockquote>
  <i>“Mine. It’s mine. You can’t leave me again. I need this. You smell so f*cking perfect. Nothing is ever going to be this damn perfect for me.” </i>
</blockquote> <br><br><br>...gotta love those <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[pregnancy <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> hormones!<br><br>There were a lot of sweet moments between them as well. I loved when he bought her the bed and the rose petals!! I also got a kick out of it when he pulled out his American Express black card! And I loved the dual POV's!<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379786887i/488833.jpg" width="350" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>Most surprising moment? When Abe talked to both Rush and Blaire. Didn't see that one coming but now that it did, I hope something more comes out of it. <br><br>The ending that didn't seem like an ending? Yea, maybe I'm just hoping but it doesn't sound like this is the end of Rush and Blaire. I'm sure we will get some of them in Woods' and Grant's books but I'm keeping my fingers crossed for another Rush and Blaire. <br><br><br>Favorite quotes:<br><br>♥ "Seeing your face. God, baby, I can’t do this. I can’t pretend I’m not f*cking thrilled you’re standing in my house right now.”<br><br>♥ “I will do anything. Anything, Blaire, just to be near you. I can’t think about anything else. I can’t focus on anything. So never think you’re inconveniencing me. You need me, I’m there.”<br><br>♥ “She’s amazing. No… she’s perfect. Everything about her is f*cking perfect,” I said aloud then shifted my gaze back to Meg. “I don’t just love her, she owns me. Completely. I’d do anything for her.”<br><br>♦ Make your move,” Woods warned. <br><br>I broke into a run. <br><br>♥ "F*ck… I was also gonna cry."</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="3677331957092268822" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16809610-beth-michele?shelf=my-favs">my-favs</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer523098280" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17344762923931419507">I loved this story, but then again I love Rush and Blaire (notice I put him first). :)<br/><br/>Where to begin. Such an honesty and sweetness to their relationship. The innocent girl from Alabama, and the bad boy son of the rocker. To me, it shouted irony. Blaire was anything but innocent given her life experiences, and Rush wasn’t so much a bad boy, as a boy with a heart, who was craving the love he never had, but always gave away. <br/><br/>I loved the way Rush cared for Blaire, how protective he was, the little </span>
  <span id="freeText17344762923931419507" style="display:none">I loved this story, but then again I love Rush and Blaire (notice I put him first). :)<br /><br />Where to begin. Such an honesty and sweetness to their relationship. The innocent girl from Alabama, and the bad boy son of the rocker. To me, it shouted irony. Blaire was anything but innocent given her life experiences, and Rush wasn’t so much a bad boy, as a boy with a heart, who was craving the love he never had, but always gave away. <br /><br />I loved the way Rush cared for Blaire, how protective he was, the little ways he showed his love for her. Need an example? He wanted to go with her to buy her a bra for heaven's sake. I mean, let's be real. Going to get sized for a new bra is not a pleasurable experience. However, sprinkle a little Rush Finlay on there, and suddenly, the experience becomes a lot more enjoyable.<br /><br />The sex was seriously hot. Seriously.<br /><br />Loved Woods and Bethy, and Grant too. Can’t wait for more of them! I have to admit I didn’t take to Woods in the first story, but I definitely did in this one. I loved how he looked after Blaire. He really cared for her. <br /><br />Overall, I loved the book, but then again I love the two of them together. You could pretty much tell me they sat together gazing into each other's eyes while slurping bowls of stringy spaghetti and I'd love it.<br /><br />Thank you Abbi Glines!!<br /><br />I only have one last thing to say...MORE please!<br /></span>

  <b> HELL YES</b>

  <b>Casting</b>

  <span id="freeText11652597655040446683" style="display:none">SPOILER FREE REVIEW <b>-mature content reader discretion is advised.</b><br>4 STARS out of 5<br>Genre: New Adult Romance<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401055ra/777797.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_miw9d9OtCs1qjslnn_zpsdc434c33.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Did I love this book?<u>
  <b> HELL YES</b>
</u>!!<br><br><br>That first chapter... WHOA! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401055ra/777798.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mdpsxsQu3b1rnxj3b_zpsc5feadde.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u>
  <b>Casting</b>
</u> -My Rush and Blaire<br><br><i>
  <b>“She’s amazing. No… she’s perfect. Everything about her is fucking perfect,”</b>
</i> I said aloud then shifted my gaze back to Meg.<i>
  <b> “I don’t just love her, she owns me. Completely. I’d do anything for her.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401055i/777799.jpg" alt=" photo 3b3b47a5-c30d-4f7e-8f48-375beb020b40_zps09e44718.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>'I couldn’t let myself believe he was my happily ever after. I was smarter than that.'</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401055i/777800.jpg" alt=" photo 91792eab-3022-4f7f-869b-076d93d59fa0_zpsdafdc586.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401055i/777801.jpg" alt=" photo COUPLESLOVE_zps96308c81.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The book starts with a shocking revelation..well maybe not that shocking. I saw it coming, but I'll be damn, reading it had me a wreck. Blaire is trying to move on with her life and being with Rush is not part of the plan.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401055ra/777802.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mglkr8AdwR1r8mmrfo1_500_zps76163c9a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is just one problem. Blaire and Rush are perfect for one another whether she wants to admit it or not, it's the truth.<br><br>It does not take long before she is back in Rosemary Beach and facing Rush <b>but press the happy brakes</b> because her reasons are not what you think.<br><br><i>
  <b>“Hello, Rush,”</b>
</i> she said, breaking the silence. The sound of her voice almost sent me to my knees. God, I’d missed her voice.<br><br>Blaire needs to make money and getting her old job back is the best option. She knows that she will have to see Rush and on top of that deal with Nan. But right now she does not care.. She's desperate. The bright side is Bethy, if she knows nothing else, she does know that Bethy has her back.<br><br>Keeping away from Rush will be pretty hard because he is hell bent on making things right. He wants Blaire back.<br><br><i>
  <b>'If I was going to ease her back into being comfortable with me I needed to calm down.'</b>
</i><br><br>She can't really fight it. And she knows it!<br><br><i>
  <b>'He was lethal to my emotions and good sense. Distance.'</b>
</i><br><br>The story takes off quickly. Blaire can't keeping fighting love. Soon her and Rush are in a heated battle. But..it's not<b>
  <i> exactly</i>
</b> what you might think.<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399854ra/774223.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mdn1frJZ3r1rygxh4_zps1418771f.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401055i/777803.jpg" alt=" photo bd0f5769-0b2d-48d3-be96-c1aece2c2cfa_zpsad7370c6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401055i/777804.jpg" alt=" photo 0c960025-d572-4f8b-81ff-8159226b013d_zps449307f7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401055ra/777805.gif" alt=" photo Iloveit_zpsc3e2b260.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So <b>H O T</b>!!<br><br>This book was PANTY MELTING<b> HOT</b>!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401056i/777806.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_mhhgf7afSZ1s4g9g0o1_500_zps4cccc426.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Winning Blaire back proves challenging. Mainly because she does not see herself fitting in to his world. <br><br><i>
  <b>“I saw him today. He was having fun. He fit in. He’s where he belongs. I’m where I belong. I don’t fit in with his world.”</b>
</i><br><br>That really pissed me off.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401056i/777807.jpg" alt=" photo cb8ef72ca1228c84b307ea72bb9d3750_zps0fed6358.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>He clears that misconception up and makes it crystal clear.<br><br><i>
  <b>“No. One. Comes. Before. You.”</b>
</i><br><br>*SWOON*<br><br>Slowly he proves that he is not going anywhere. He proves that he loves her. And a second chance is rewarded.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401056ra/777808.gif" alt=" photo LOVE-WONTLETYOUDOTHISGIF_zpsa177644e.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Then tragedy strikes.<br><br><br><u>
  <b>FAVORITES </b>
</u><br><b>My favorite Lines, scenes and/or characters</b><br><br><u>Lines that made me laugh out loud</u><br><i>
  <b>“He’s your man. Say it because it’s true. The guy worships at your altar.”</b>

</b><br><br><br><u>My Thoughts</u><br>I loved it!   <b>LOVE LOVE LOVE LOVE LOVED THIS ONE !! ♥♥♥♥♥</b>
</i><br/><br/> Never Too Far picks 3 weeks after Rush and Blaire said goodbye to each other ( my heart still hearts from that goodbye) and both Blaire and Rush are Miserable ( so am I since they are not together..). Blaire felt betrayed by Rush because he withheld information from her about her dad, mom, and Nan..<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401297ra/778748.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>

  <span id="freeText715021745739824975" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>LOVE LOVE LOVE LOVE LOVED THIS ONE !! ♥♥♥♥♥</b>
</i><br><br> Never Too Far picks 3 weeks after Rush and Blaire said goodbye to each other ( my heart still hearts from that goodbye) and both Blaire and Rush are Miserable ( so am I since they are not together..). Blaire felt betrayed by Rush because he withheld information from her about her dad, mom, and Nan..<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401297ra/778748.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b>Blaire has gone back to Sweet Home Alabama to nurse her wounds.. then she gets a bomb dropped on her..</b>
</i> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401265ra/778585.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Blaire ends up going back to Florida where Rush is and the only friends she has.. she still loves Rush and she's going to need him, but she's determined to keep him at a distance.</i> <br><br><i>
  <b> Rush is having none of that though and trys to break down her defenses at every oppurtunity.. with a lot of this... </b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401297ra/778749.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>Rush is really good at several things by the way...he has a tongue ring..</b>
</i><br><br><i>
  <b>Rush screws up constantly!!! Never meaning to.. but he pissed me off so many times I wanted to reach in my Kindle and kick his ass for being so dumb dumb DUMB!!!</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397452ra/766922.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Through all of Rush's screw ups though.. I still loved him.. and he and Blaire both needed each other so badly. Her father is a screw up, his sister is a total bitch.. they have so many obsiticals... but one thing will bind them forever and they have to go through so much to get to that special place.. but when they do--- its beautiful<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395750ra/762292.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b> Loved this book so much..... it totally lived up to the hype!<br><br>My ONLY fault with this book is there was NO F'KING EPILOGUE!!!! WE ARE JUST CUT OFF WITH A NICE FINAL SCENE AND THEN BOOM.. NO EPILOGUE.... WTF???? I NEED AN EPILOGUE PRONTO!!!<br><br>Click here to see Never Too Far's bonus chapter that Abbi has given us<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.abbiglines.com/2013/03/673/">http://www.abbiglines.com/2013/03/673/</a><br><br><br><b>NEWEST INFO!!!! ABBI IS MAKING ANOTHER BOOK FOR RUSH AND BLAIRE!!!<b><br>The End<br><br> </b></b></b>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="715021745739824975" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
