<div id="review_478787119" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/478787119" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/478787119?book_show_action=true">Dec 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer478787119" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16172134977910342744"><b>
  <u> 5 Amazing Rush Crush Stars!!!</u>
</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“I don’t just love her, she owns me. Completely. I’d do anything for her.”</i>
</b> <br/>I have been waiting for this sequel for almost 5 months... For those of you who have read Fallen Too Far, you know how brutal the cliffhanger was. Everything was a mess. I was heartbroken. I was so excited to read this one, too hopefully see everything come together. And I LOVED IT! <br/><br/><b>RUSH</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/0a55173b-3561-43fd-a49c-08db4aeef4fa_zpsafc80a02.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401038i/777727.jpg' alt=' photo 0a55173b-3561-43fd-a49c-08db4aeef4fa_zpsafc80a02.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>“I’ll be whatever you allow me to be, Blaire. Just do’t shut me out again. Please.”</b><br/><br/><b>BLAIRE</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/71b66391-46d4-4cd6-ba94-29aa8e274571_zpsaf343ecf.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401038i/777728.jpg' alt=' photo 71b66391-46d4-4cd6-ba94-29aa8e274571_zpsaf343ecf.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>I </b></span>
  <span id="freeText16172134977910342744" style="display:none"><b>
  <u> 5 Amazing Rush Crush Stars!!!</u>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“I don’t just love her, she owns me. Completely. I’d do anything for her.”</i>
</b> <br>I have been waiting for this sequel for almost 5 months... For those of you who have read Fallen Too Far, you know how brutal the cliffhanger was. Everything was a mess. I was heartbroken. I was so excited to read this one, too hopefully see everything come together. And I LOVED IT! <br><br><b>RUSH</b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/0a55173b-3561-43fd-a49c-08db4aeef4fa_zpsafc80a02.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401038i/777727.jpg" alt=" photo 0a55173b-3561-43fd-a49c-08db4aeef4fa_zpsafc80a02.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>“I’ll be whatever you allow me to be, Blaire. Just do’t shut me out again. Please.”</b><br><br><b>BLAIRE</b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/71b66391-46d4-4cd6-ba94-29aa8e274571_zpsaf343ecf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401038i/777728.jpg" alt=" photo 71b66391-46d4-4cd6-ba94-29aa8e274571_zpsaf343ecf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>I needed for us to move on. But maybe I never would. I’d always have a reminder of Rush.</b><br><br>Never Too Far picked up right where Fallen Too Far left off... Blaire is broken hearted and devastated, back in Alabama staying with Cain’s grandmother. Rush is desperate and hopeless without Blaire. He never thought he would fall in love, and now that he has and he can’t have her, he is just lost. Blaire’s friend Bethy comes to town and talks Blaire into coming back to Rosemary. Blaire has a plan. She will go back to work at the club for Woods, save some money, and in a few months she will be able to start fresh. Somewhere else. She knows seeing Rush will be unavoidable, but they can never be more than friends. With all the family drama, plus a new complication that Blaire is keeping secret, it just won’t work. She has to do what is best, she has something bigger than herself to think about now. When Rush finds out Blaire is back for a while, he will do anything to get her back and keep her with him. <br><b>
  <i> “I will do anything. Anything, Blaire, just to be near you. I can’t think about anything else.”</i>
</b><br>He is a man on a mission. After a while, Blaire cannot resist Rush Finlay. Not only does Blaire have a secret, but there is even more family secrets/drama between these two...<br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/f77ce6d0-b9b4-4b86-b8b9-9722798bcb78_zps3c73ece8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401038i/777729.jpg" alt=" photo f77ce6d0-b9b4-4b86-b8b9-9722798bcb78_zps3c73ece8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>It took me a while to warm up to Rush in Fallen Too Far, but not in this one. Rush is so in love and willing to do anything for Blaire. He is more emotional and sentimental in this one, but he is still a hot as hell alpha man too! Best of both worlds! <br>I’m happy Blaire was able to move forward. I was nervous towards the beginning she wouldn’t be able to. She felt all alone in the world, but she really did have more than a few people who love her and care for her and I was glad she realized that. I was also happy that her dad talked to her, that conversation was crazy- but she needed to know it.<br><br>There were so many great secondary characters- Woods and Bethy! Loved them both! I am so excited about Woods book :D He was really great, there for Blaire in the way she needed him without being pushy. Bethy is just an all around great friend to Blaire, plus she is a hoot! I was a little disappointed with Grant in this book, seeing as how much I loved him in the first. Nan was pretty terrible, but that is to be expected. I wish we could witness when she learns the truth. Ugh- what a bitch. Rush’s mom wasn’t really in this one, but I still hate her lol. <br><br>I really don’t think it is possible for Abbi Glines to write a book that I don’t love! After being up almost 24 straight hours, I stayed up and read this... Once I started it, it was impossible to put down! I enjoyed every second of this book! A fabulous story with characters you will fall in love with all over again! If you haven’t read these books- you are missing out!!!<br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/d981f30e-d247-4e47-a079-c22a9539b4ef_zpsbfd242cf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401038i/777730.jpg" alt=" photo d981f30e-d247-4e47-a079-c22a9539b4ef_zpsbfd242cf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>“No man has ever loved a woman as much as I love you. Nothing will ever come before you.”</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16172134977910342744" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer480331857" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer647205005494394306"><b>4 Crush-On-Rush (but kinda mad at him) Stars<br/><br/><i>"You only deserve what you make yourself worthy of. Do what I couldn’t. Be a man.”</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401265i/778588._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='180' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>There are some blows that a person isn't capable of handling. A breaking point to sanity. Some truths are not meant to be acknowledged...<br/><br/>Blaine's whole world just crashed. She was settled, at peace and loved. She had Rush and she had a chance in a new life.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401265i/778582._SX540_.png' width='400' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>But the unexpected truth of her parents' past and Nan, the secret all knew but no one bothered to share with her, has</span>
  <span id="freeText647205005494394306" style="display:none"><b>4 Crush-On-Rush (but kinda mad at him) Stars<br><br><i>"You only deserve what you make yourself worthy of. Do what I couldn’t. Be a man.”</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401265i/778588._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are some blows that a person isn't capable of handling. A breaking point to sanity. Some truths are not meant to be acknowledged...<br><br>Blaine's whole world just crashed. She was settled, at peace and loved. She had Rush and she had a chance in a new life.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401265i/778582._SX540_.png" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But the unexpected truth of her parents' past and Nan, the secret all knew but no one bothered to share with her, has her running away, hurt, confused and pregnant. But Alabama isn't the home she knew anymore and she can't hide from Rush forever. She has to face reality, fight for what she deserves, confront Rush and deal with the people that betrayed her. Will she be strong enough to leave the past behind? Will she emerge a winner and give herself at chance at happiness and love?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400461i/776070.jpg" width="400" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Rush has never loved before. But Blaire is worth the effort. Destroyed and confused, angry at himself and the people and circumstance that drove her away, he will have to beg and plead and fight her tooth and nail. If he doesn't screw up everything again.<br><br><b>
  <i>“She’s amazing. No… she’s perfect. Everything about her is fucking perfect,” I said aloud then shifted my gaze back to Meg. “I don’t just love her, she owns me. Completely. I’d do anything for her.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382030895i/5596113._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If Book#1 messed with my heart, this one pretty much shred it...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380384773ra/743412.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>These two kids mess up and screw their lives. Make bad decisions and fuck up. I swear to God, by the end of the book I wanted to throttle Rush, smother him with kisses, smack him and love him to death...<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401265ra/778590.gif" width="245" height="184" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><i>Special Mentions:</i> Woods, I'm totally in love with you... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401265ra/778591.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nan... you uppity bitch...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397452ra/766922.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My feelings aside, I really think that these books are awesome. Emotional and real, raw and heartbreaking. A beautiful story of a truly beautiful couple.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401265i/778592._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And if you are already craving more there is a bonus chapter just for you:<br><br><a href="http://www.abbiglines.com/2013/03/673/" rel="nofollow noopener">NEVER TOO FAR - The Bonus Chapter</a><br><br><b>THANK YOU GOD!!!! I managed to wait for this book to be released and I enjoyed the hell out of this back to back reading.</b><br><br><i>My reaction, to the release news:<br><br>March 2013</i><br>Early release, my wonderful ladies.. ENJOY!!<br>You did it! You survived the cliffhanger!!! <br><br>And I kinda cheated it, too... LOL!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/546264.gif" width="500" height="226" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/478720934?book_show_action=true">Dec 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura&#39;s Book Addiction" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura&#39;s Book Addiction" href="/user/show/3551390-laura-s-book-addiction">Laura&#39;s Book Addiction</a>

        rated it

<div id="review_489162762" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/489162762" />
    <a title="Miss H" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15490946-miss-h"><img alt="Miss H" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475977422p2/15490946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/489162762?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Miss H" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Miss H" href="/user/show/15490946-miss-h">Miss H</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17447928-never-too-far">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=hated-this-book">hated-this-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=insufferable-mc">insufferable-mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=badly-written">badly-written</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=smutty-reads">smutty-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=douch-canoe-hero">douch-canoe-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=kill-it-with-fire">kill-it-with-fire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=everyone-else-loves-it">everyone-else-loves-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=please-fire-your-editor">please-fire-your-editor</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer489162762" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17161084999485882709"><b>Warning: spoilers abound.</b><br/><br/>Well, I’ll start off by saying that I didn’t hate the entire book, but I hated enough of it to warrant the 1-star rating I feel it deserves. I mean, it had its moments, sure, but for the most part, the bad far outweighed the good. Perhaps I came into the second book with too high hopes. Maybe my expectations were too high. Suffice it to say, I was sorely disappointed.<br/><br/>Never Too Far can be summed up in one word: boring.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470501840ra/19935958.gif' width='400' height='168' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><br/>Much like the first book, Fallen Too Far, lack of pro</span>
  <span id="freeText17161084999485882709" style="display:none"><b>Warning: spoilers abound.</b><br><br>Well, I’ll start off by saying that I didn’t hate the entire book, but I hated enough of it to warrant the 1-star rating I feel it deserves. I mean, it had its moments, sure, but for the most part, the bad far outweighed the good. Perhaps I came into the second book with too high hopes. Maybe my expectations were too high. Suffice it to say, I was sorely disappointed.<br><br>Never Too Far can be summed up in one word: boring.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470501840ra/19935958.gif" width="400" height="168" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>Much like the first book, Fallen Too Far, lack of proper editing was an issue for me. There’s still the problem of missing commas and incorrect dialogue punctuation, along with a host of other problems.<br><br>My biggest complaint with the first book was Rush himself. I thought he was an inconsiderate jerk and some other not-so-nice things. However, this time around, my contempt has now shifted to Blaire. She got on my nerves and frustrated me beyond measure. She was a martyr to the extreme. For someone who claimed to be so independent, she sure was dependent on a lot of people. She talked a big game, going on and on about how she planned to start over someplace new, but not once did she actually do, well, anything. She made no effort toward her proposed plans. It was nothing more than an empty and half-hearted desire. She was all talk and no action. Everyone liked her, everyone wanted to protect her, and everyone wanted to help her out in one way or another. And she had no problem letting them. She was too nice, too forgiving, and too understanding. I wanted to shake some sense into her. She was a complete Mary-Sue at times—that is to say, when she wasn’t busy being a hypocrite. She was quick to make assumptions and jump to conclusions. She had no self-confidence, which I found extremely irritating. She was a doormat and just plain weak. It's hard for me to root for a character like that.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402579ra/782581.gif" width="400" height="224" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As for Rush, I don’t know what happened to his character. He was a completely different person, and I don’t mean that as a compliment. I wasn’t a fan of alternating points of view. I could’ve done without Rush’s point of view altogether. It’s just that I found his thought process to be too unrealistic for a guy. He over-analyzed everything, constantly worried that he would somehow upset Blaire. Then again, she didn’t make it easy on him. She misinterpreted everything he said and didn’t believe him, no matter how earnest he was. Of course, this was before he proved himself a liar when he promised Blaire that she would always come first in his life. He was overly emotional and whiny and second-guessed himself far too often. Then, on top of everything else, he got sappy. As a result, when he acted like a possessive, alpha male, I couldn't take him seriously.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402579i/782582.jpg" width="397" height="272" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Don’t even get me started on the drama involving Nan. The entire situation grated on my last nerve. Every time things would start to settle, something would happen involving her, and we’d be right back where we started. I understand Nan and Rush are close, but she’s no longer a child; she’s a grown woman. So she has daddy issues. Guess what? My give a damn’s busted. Get over it. Rush enabled her and treated her as if she were a delicate flower. I got tired of Rush (and Grant) making excuses for her behavior. <br><br>I want my time back. If I could unread this book, I would. It was longer than it needed to be, and for a book with very little plot, it dragged on and on. The repetitive miscommunication and misunderstandings drove me to the brink of madness. They were blown way out of proportion, all for the sake of creating drama, because the plot had nothing driving it. The secondary characters only made an appearance when they could be used as a tool to stir up more drama. It lulled because not even the not-so-shocking pregnancy or Nan's accident were enough to keep things interesting. It was beyond predictable and poorly plotted.<br><br>Sorry, but an excessive amount of smut does not make up for lack of plot and character development. Rush and Blaire used sex as a substitute for talking out feelings and working out problems far too often. Rush was more or less Blaire’s human sex toy. To be honest, Rush and Blaire's relationship still makes no sense to me. I have no idea what they see in each other. They haven't had enough time to truly get to know one another, and now with the pregnancy, things are more rushed than ever. <br><br>Also, that ending…yeah. Talk about abrupt. Not that I wanted to waste any more of my time, but seriously, an epilogue would’ve been nice.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17161084999485882709" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer12360520796034366656"> I read book 1 on a whim actually and I should have checked first if it was a series because I usually don't like reading a book if it's a series when the first book is a cliffhanger. I'm half regretting my choice because I'm still heartbroken from the ending of book 1. I hope time flies faster because right now I couldn't get "Fallen Too Far" out of my head.<br/><br/>OMG, it's there already. Can't wait to go get it!<br/><br/><b>UPDATED February 27, 2013</b><br/>Okay.This was me... <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/464171.gif' width='150' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/> I was practically dancing around my room on</span>
  <span id="freeText12360520796034366656" style="display:none"> I read book 1 on a whim actually and I should have checked first if it was a series because I usually don't like reading a book if it's a series when the first book is a cliffhanger. I'm half regretting my choice because I'm still heartbroken from the ending of book 1. I hope time flies faster because right now I couldn't get "Fallen Too Far" out of my head.<br><br>OMG, it's there already. Can't wait to go get it!<br><br><b>UPDATED February 27, 2013</b><br>Okay.This was me... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/464171.gif" width="150" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br> I was practically dancing around my room once I finally got the book.<br><br><br>It took me 4 hours to finish reading the book and totally worth my lack of sleep the next day.<br><br><b>“No. One. Comes. Before. You.”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1356822956l/17029526.jpg" width="300" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I still can't decide if this should be rated as 4.5 stars or a perfect 5, still the rating is pretty so I don't think there's a problem in that score.<br><br>I love this book as much as I love the first book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16070903.Fallen_Too_Far" rel="nofollow noopener">Fallen Too Far</a>. <br><br>Three weeks have passed since the ending of the first book. <br><br><b>"It had been three weeks, four days and twelve hours since I’d seen her." ~Rush</b><br><br>(Hilarious, how he knows the exact time since he last saw her.)<br><br>It tells both the POV of both Rush and Blaire's which I totally love.<br><br>I both love and hate how the story goes in terms on how their relationship progressed, still my love for this book was higher than my hate for it.<br><br>I guess if you read the book, you'd understand why I hate it at the same time. <br><br>Rush totally understands how to handle things when it comes to getting Blaire back and I love him for that. He knows what to do but in some instances there was just some hurdles he needs to overcome (with his relationship to Nan and what happened at the near ending --&gt; which he did thanks to an inspiration or a push by a certain person in other terms Abe, Blaire's father). <br><br>Speaking of Blaire's father, that was another shocking truth wherein they wouldn't have these problems in the first place if it weren't for the lies of Georgina (I really hate her! She's my number one and number two would be Nan).<br><br>Now, sweet Blaire. As much as I love her too, I hated the part where she had a lot of insecurities. I mean, I understand why but seriously she looks down on herself too much. She also misinterprets a lot of things that involved Rush wherein Rush had to grovel. Though, what surprised me is her acceptance towards her father at the end in which I'm happy too.<br><br>The father of Blaire is a weak man but I'm glad that he helped both Rush and Blaire in way. Also, how he truly feels for his family. <br><br>Once again, I gotta say I totally love this book. <br><br>Like they also said,<b>"YOU CAN NEVER HAVE ENOUGH OF RUSH FINLAY"</b>!<br><br>I'm happy that it's the end but I wish there was an epilogue. I wasn't contented in the ending. <br><br>Something I just want to mention about. I can't wait for Woods' story in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17333880-twisted-perfection" rel="nofollow noopener">Twisted Perfection</a>. I'm also happy that it's only in one book but guess what? I'm not sure if I'm gonna be happy with Grant's story. <br><br></span>

<div id="review_509194469" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/509194469" />
    <a title="Autumn Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6908049-autumn-review"><img alt="Autumn Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1399327915p2/6908049.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/509194469?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Autumn Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Autumn Review" href="/user/show/6908049-autumn-review">Autumn Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6908049-autumn-review?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6908049-autumn-review?shelf=review">review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6908049-autumn-review?shelf=beta">beta</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer509194469" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8810422269385434198">Well, Abbi Glines has done it again. She gave me another book that I fell in love with. Sequels are often hard to write, but Rush and Blaire had more to tell. I was thrilled with the outcome and I can't wait for everyone to read this, so I can talk about it with someone! There is so much I want to say, but I don't want to ruin the story for you. <br/><br/>I still love all the key players in the story. By the end of Fallen Too Far, I did love Rush. It took me a while to warm up to him, but in this one, I r</span>
  <span id="freeText8810422269385434198" style="display:none">Well, Abbi Glines has done it again. She gave me another book that I fell in love with. Sequels are often hard to write, but Rush and Blaire had more to tell. I was thrilled with the outcome and I can't wait for everyone to read this, so I can talk about it with someone! There is so much I want to say, but I don't want to ruin the story for you. <br /><br />I still love all the key players in the story. By the end of Fallen Too Far, I did love Rush. It took me a while to warm up to him, but in this one, I really fell hard. He is determined to win Blaire back. He truly feels remorse over hurting her. And Blaire...I still like her. She has to make some difficult decisions in this book. I felt like she handled them very realistically. She didn't jump in blindly. I still love Grant and anxiously await his story. Nan is still a brat, but we start to understand her a bit better. But the character I loved getting to see more of in this book was Woods. I was on the fence about Woods in the first book, but let me tell you...he will steal your heart in this one, if he hasn't already. He's a great guy. <br /><br />If you've read Fallen Too Far, you know how it ended. Major life altering secrets were revealed and it tested Blaire and Rush's relationship. What I loved about Never Too Far was that it took time for Blaire to even want to talk to Rush. His betrayal wasn't easily forgotten. Well, now Blaire has her own secrets and she isn't the only one. Everything I thought I knew, was wrong. Glines threw me for a loop a few times in this book. <br /><br />Overall, I loved it, but you probably aren't surprised. There are some major things happening in this book and I promise you, you will be enthralled until the end. Blaire and Rush's love for each other was addicting. If you thought they had steam in the first book, just wait. This one is even hotter. The ending was absolutely perfect for them. This book also gives a good lead in to Woods' story, Twisted Perfection. If you want romance, steam, drama, and a great love story, you must check this series out. <br /><br />*You will need to read Fallen Too Far before you start this one.*<br /><br />Favorite Quote:<br />~"No man has ever loved a woman as much as I love you. Nothing will ever come before you. I don't know what else I have to do to prove it to you but I won't let you down again. I won't hurt you. You don't have to be alone anymore. I need you."-Loc2416</span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14477213594135797023"><b>** 3.5 Rush-Crush Stars**</b><br/><br/>I could literally slap myself for waiting this long to write my review.<br/>That being said, I'm gonna keep this short and ever so sweet.<br/><br/><br/><b>"It had been three weeks, four days and twelve hours since I'd seen her. Since she'd torn my heart out." </b><br/><br/><br/>I feel your pain Rush! <br/>But now the wait is over for both of us!<br/><br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401130ra/778073.gif' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/>I loved Fallen too Far .<br/><br/>It is one of my favorite books so you can't imagine how excited I was to read this book. <br/><br/>Boy, I didn't know I was in for a big surprise.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401130ra/778074.gif' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>And it's not a</b></span>
  <span id="freeText14477213594135797023" style="display:none"><b>** 3.5 Rush-Crush Stars**</b><br><br>I could literally slap myself for waiting this long to write my review.<br>That being said, I'm gonna keep this short and ever so sweet.<br><br><br><b>"It had been three weeks, four days and twelve hours since I'd seen her. Since she'd torn my heart out." </b><br><br><br>I feel your pain Rush! <br>But now the wait is over for both of us!<br><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401130ra/778073.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>I loved Fallen too Far .<br><br>It is one of my favorite books so you can't imagine how excited I was to read this book. <br><br>Boy, I didn't know I was in for a big surprise.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401130ra/778074.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>And it's not a pleasant one, mind you.</b><br><br><br><br><br>So how can a book almost made me want to massacre our whole neighborhood? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401130ra/778075.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>One word: <b>BLAIRE </b>.<br><br><br><br>So, Blaire is pregnant and dealing with it.<br><br>Rush is dealing with the loss of Blaire. <br><br>There are external characters, like Nan, Grant , Cain, Woods, but other than that, there really isn’t a story line.<br><br><br>All the time, Blaire is like a freaking bomb that will eventually blows off everyone’s asses! <br><br><br>I understand she’s pregnant and she’s emotional.<br><br>But God, there’s just no excuse for this. Being pregnant doesn’t make you brain dead! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/381074.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fine, you have an issue with the guy who knocked you off, big deal!<br>But the baby has nothing to do with your fucked up life!<br><br>And, she planned on not telling him about her pregnancy at first because she thinks she can take care of the baby without Rush’ help.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380365299ra/717232.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Fuck it! </b><br>That is just the stupidest thing I’ve ever read!<br><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401130ra/778076.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>So,time for more <b>RUSH...</b><br><br><br>I really felt bad for Rush because this book is not really a big picnic for him.<br><br>He does all the chasing.<br><br>He does all the things to make their relationship work.<br><br>Hell, he is even willing to sacrifice his family for Blaire. <br><br>But every time he does a small mistake, Blaire goes all overly-dramatic and threatens to leave again.<br><br>The more I read I just felt like I was in bad game of ping pong.<br><br>Back and forth...back and forth, Blaire and Rush went.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401130ra/778077.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br>COME ON!<br>Fuck that shit!<br>Give the guy a fucking break! <br><br><br><br>Hmmm...<br>Moving on to:<br><br>Blaire's father, who drops a bomb and I thought...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401130ra/778078.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br>Nonetheless, this book is also very steamy! <br>They are so passionate about each other that the pages burn every time they are together! <br><b>Rush is a sex god!<br> <br>Period.<br> <br>There I said it! </b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401130ra/778079.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>As my above ranting proves, Blaire irritated the living daylight's out of me, but the redeeming factor was hot, protective and utterly gorgeous Rush.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401130ra/778080.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Also, was it me or did the ending seemed "rush"ed ? <br><br>Sure there’s another book in the works on Blaire and Rush (from what I read), but I just feel like everything should have been wrapped up in this one. <br><br><br>I know I am ranting, maybe because I am angry I waited so long and maybe my high expectations.<br><br>With everything said, book 3 better be darn good. <br><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401130ra/778081.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br><i>Special Mentions: </i><br><br>Woods, I'm totally in love with you...<br>The only thing and I mean only thing I liked was Woods and THANK GOD, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17333880.Twisted_Perfection__Perfection___1_" title="Twisted Perfection (Perfection, #1) by Abbi Glines" rel="nofollow noopener">Twisted Perfection</a> is his story. <br><br>I did enjoy it but I cannot say that I am in love with this book like I hoped I would.<br><br>If you read my review of Fallen Too Far you would have seen how excited and how messed up it left me.<br>With Never Too Far I am left feeling...<br><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401130ra/778082.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>So, yeah, this pretty much sums it up.<br><br></span>

pregnant and with all the people knowing in their small town she needs to leave before it will show.<br>She came back to Rosemary and have to inform Rush that she will be staying for a while in a condo she and Bethy will share,and get back to work to save up before she will leave for good.With her morning ickness and Rush sticking up with her and all their family drama.Blaire was torn between her love for Rush and his priority to his family....<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407124ra/794919.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img think about anything else.I cant focus on anything.So never think you're inconveniencing me.You need me,I'm there"!!</b><br><br><br>This book was addictive!!!<br>I fell in love with Blaire and Rush from the moment I met them back in Fallen Too Far.I loved watching their relationship evolve and the way their story paned out.Never Too Far was jam packed with emotion,love and some serious steamy personality and you’ve got one sexy hero!!I absolutely LOVED just how protective he was over Blaire. He didn’t stop at anything to get his girl back!!!!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393650i/757915._SY540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br> <br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407124ra/794921.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>This books is also very steamy!   <span id="freeText2385508785083626602" style="display:none"><b>3.5-4 Stars!!!</b><br /><br />I really enjoyed this book. I love Rush!!! He is so sexy!!! I can't get enough of his dirty mouth.         <a title="The Romance Book Disciple (Samantha)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="The Romance Book Disciple (Samantha)" href="/user/show/3009708-the-romance-book-disciple-samantha">The Romance Book Disciple (Samantha)</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1649004807" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8343373542689392604">Another one I gobbled up in a few hours! This books are New Adult drama at its most Springer worthy! Rush is a giant effing tool and a total moron. If Blaire had any other options in the world, she would have left his dumb ass. But, with no parents, and only a handful of friends, she is pretty much stuck sleeping on the floor (because she can't afford a bed), walking 3.5 miles (because she can't afford a car), and having to apply for medicare to pay for her doctors visits. Meanwhile, Rush has 4 </span>
  <span id="freeText8343373542689392604" style="display:none">Another one I gobbled up in a few hours! This books are New Adult drama at its most Springer worthy! Rush is a giant effing tool and a total moron. If Blaire had any other options in the world, she would have left his dumb ass. But, with no parents, and only a handful of friends, she is pretty much stuck sleeping on the floor (because she can't afford a bed), walking 3.5 miles (because she can't afford a car), and having to apply for medicare to pay for her doctors visits. Meanwhile, Rush has 4 cars, a giant house with beds in every room, and has never given money a second thought. The disparity between the 2 is striking, but it makes me even more irritated with Rush for not even wondering what her life is like. He never bothers to ask and then is shocked when he finds out she had to walk 3 miles because he left her standing in the driveway without a key to get in, or that she was sleeping on a friends couch and then eventually on the floor because she literally has NOTHING. Like, dude, you know what she has been through, how is it you keep missing this shit!?<br />And what the fuck is up with Grant? Sometimes he is Team Nan then he does a 180 and is Team Blaire. His mood swings are giving me whiplash. </span>
  <a data-text-id="8343373542689392604" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

Then she died and I moved. I got my heart and world shattered and came home. You've been here for me. </b></span>
  <span id="freeText8839841647080762068" style="display:none"><b> Two Weeks Late.....</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401650i/779823.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Just when Blaire thought she had let Rush go, there she is back in Sumit where she discovers she's pregnant.<br>She has a confrontation with Caine..<br><br><b>“I’m not sure what exactly you think we’ve been through. We were best friends, then we were a couple, then my momma got sick and you needed your dick sucked so you cheated on me. I took care of my sick momma alone. No one to lean on. Then she died and I moved. I got my heart and world shattered and came home. You've been here for me. I didn’t ask you to but you have. I’m thankful for that but it doesn’t make all that other stuff go away. It doesn’t make up for the fact you deserted me when I needed you the most. So excuse me if when my world is once again about to be jerked out from under me that you aren’t the first person I run to. You haven’t earned that yet" </b><br><br>Pregnant with Rush's baby... So now she has no where to go, no family or money... Things are not looking bright for Blaire... <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401650i/779824._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>She finds herself back in the same town where Rush and Nan are.. Can she stay or should she go? She decides to stay for a while with Bethy and work again at the country club until she's saved enough to leave... <br><br>Rush....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401650i/779825._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Still Broken that his love Blaire left... Secrets and lies destroyed them... He couldn't let her go, he didn't want to let her go...<br><br><b>“She wouldn't come back. She hated me. She hated Nan. She hated my mom. She hated her father. She wouldn't come back here... but God, I wanted her to.” </b><br><br><b>“It had been three weeks, four days and twelve hours since I'd seen her. Since she'd torn my heart out. If I had been drinking, I'd blame it on the alcohol. It had to be an illusion, a desperate one. But I hadn't been drinking. Not a drop. There was no mistaking Blaire. It was her. She was actually here. Blaire was back in Rosemary. She was at my house.” </b><br><br><br>Once Blaire returns Rush makes it his mission to be back in her life... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401650i/779826.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Blaire is torn... What to do? To tell Rush or not...? She decided she wouldn't tell him just yet.. He hurt her too much.. She lost everything she ever cared for. They only thing which mattered is her unborn child. Bethy helps Blaire.. Pregnancy hormones are raging, morning sickness is getting to her.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401650i/779827.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let me just say that Blaire's pregnancy hormones are crazy!!! Rush warns her to back off!!<br><br><b>“Don’t assume I’m bluffing Nan. Because this time you’ve fucked with something I care about. This affects me, so listen and shut the hell up” </b><br><br><b>“She’s back to find out where she fits and what to do next.         <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/479074150?book_show_action=true">Dec 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elizabeth (Liz)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elizabeth (Liz)" href="/user/show/5495317-elizabeth-liz">Elizabeth (Liz)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer479074150" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6427707821502910617">Review posted at: <a href='http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Swept Away By Romance</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>4 Stars<br/><br/>Never Too Far is the much-anticipated sequel to Abbi Glines' Fallen Too Far. It is a continuation of Blair and Rush's love story, and picks up immediately after Fallen Too Far ends. <br/><br/> Never Too Far has been causing quite a stir! Polarizing viewpoints and social-media hullabaloos aside, the only basis on which I am able to personally give my opinion is the story itself. Admittedly, I was one of those people anxiously awaiting the continuation of Rush a</span>
  <span id="freeText6427707821502910617" style="display:none">Review posted at: <a href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Swept Away By Romance</a><br /><br /><br /><br />4 Stars<br /><br />Never Too Far is the much-anticipated sequel to Abbi Glines' Fallen Too Far. It is a continuation of Blair and Rush's love story, and picks up immediately after Fallen Too Far ends. <br /><br /> Never Too Far has been causing quite a stir! Polarizing viewpoints and social-media hullabaloos aside, the only basis on which I am able to personally give my opinion is the story itself. Admittedly, I was one of those people anxiously awaiting the continuation of Rush and Blair's story. What would happen? How would it end? I could not wait to find out!<br /><br />Without giving anything away, I was, for the most part, happy with the way the story played out. Blair and Rush faced a life-changing decision. Yes, some of their actions during this time were stupid and immature, but they're very young. And, being very young, they are, by definition, stupid and immature;) That's kind of part of the fun, the attraction, of reading *anything* in the New Adult genre, for goodness sake! In the end, though, they both find their way...stumbling and bumbling over hurdles as they go. The ending brought a tear to my eye and a lump to my throat. I'm a sap. I have no shame about that fact;) <br /><br />Woods!!! I cannot tell you how READY I am for the great and mighty Woods to get his story (or stories)! He grew on me in Fallen Too Far. In Never Too Far, I fell head over teakettle for this SUPER SEXY and (surprise!) totally decent guy! You will LOVE Woods!!<br /><br />Sooo, is Never Too Far a literary masterpiece? Nope. If you go in expecting that, I'm not certain you've been paying attention;) At the other extreme, is this the worst book ever written? Not even close. So, where does it fall? It falls where most Abbi Glines books do for me. It falls in the 'DON'T TAKE IT TOO SERIOUSLY AND HAVE SOME FUN' category!! As I've said before, Abbi's books are one of my ultimate guilty pleasures. Fantastic character chemistry will oftentimes wipe out other negatives for me, and, in my opinion, this author writes chemistry like few others. I find Abbi Glines, as a storyteller, terribly appealing. I lose myself in the characters. The good AND the obnoxious. I laugh. I smile. I quiver. I curse (yes, I talk to the characters!). I may shed a tear on occasion. I even roll my eyes once in a while. I LOVE *all* of those things. I feel involved. I become part of the story. <br /><br />I need to warn, for those who are not fond of multi-part stories, these aren't the books for you. Fallen Too Far was never marketed as a stand-alone story. It's well-known as being just the opposite, in fact. For myself and many other fans of Rush, Blair and ALL of the characters in this series, we'll happily take as many books as Abbi Glines wants to write! I'm ready for MORE! I guarantee I'm not alone :-)</span>
  <a data-text-id="6427707821502910617" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }

      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked

    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {

    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer873750186128767376">Abbi Glines is a #1 New York Times, USA Today, and Wall Street Journal bestselling author of the Rosemary Beach, Sea Breeze, Vincent Boys, Field Party and Existence series. She never cooks unless baking during the Christmas holiday counts. She believes in ghosts and has a habit of asking people if their house is haunted before she goes in it. She drinks afternoon tea because she wants to be Britis</span>
  <span id="freeText873750186128767376" style="display:none">Abbi Glines is a #1 New York Times, USA Today, and Wall Street Journal bestselling author of the Rosemary Beach, Sea Breeze, Vincent Boys, Field Party and Existence series. She never cooks unless baking during the Christmas holiday counts. She believes in ghosts and has a habit of asking people if their house is haunted before she goes in it. She drinks afternoon tea because she wants to be British but alas she was born in Alabama. When asked how many books she has written she has to stop and count on her fingers. When she’s not locked away writing, she is reading, shopping (major shoe and purse addiction), sneaking off to the movies alone, and listening to the drama in her teenagers lives while making mental notes on the good stuff to use later. Don’t judge.<br /><br />You can connect with Abbi online in several different ways. She uses social media to procrastinate.<br /></span>
